               Seniors Celebrate Thesis Submissions with Minimal Pomp and Circumstance
              </a>
             </h1>
             <div>
              <div class="contributor-container">
               <span class="byline">
                <a href="/writer/1215811/Alex_M._Koller/" to="/writer/1215811/Alex_M._Koller/">
                 Alex M. Koller
                </a>
                and
                <a href="/writer/1215499/Taylor_C._Peterman/" to="/writer/1215499/Taylor_C._Peterman/">
                 Taylor C. Peterman
                </a>
               </span>
              </div>
              
             </div>
             <p>
              For members of the Class of 2021, virtual thesis submission is the latest in a string of quintessential experiences at the College that have been blighted by Covid-19. Though the College invited seniors to live on campus in the spring, not all opted to do so, and large social gatherings remain prohibited.
             </p>

              </a>
             </h1>
             <div>
              <div class="contributor-container">
               <span class="byline">

                </a>
                and

                </a>
               </span>
              </div>
              
             </div>
             <p>
              The Coalition for a Diverse Harvard  an alumni group centered on increasing diversity and promoting equity at the University  endorsed five candidates for this years Board of Overseers election and six candidates for elected directorships on the board of the Harvard Alumni Association on Wednesday.
             </p>

               Bacow Defends Harvards Tenure Process Following Cornel Wests Decision to Depart
              </a>
             </h1>
             <div>
              <div class="contributor-container">
               <span class="byline">
                <a href="/writer/1215368/Jasper_G._Goodman/" to="/writer/1215368/Jasper_G._Goodman/">

                </a>
               </span>

             </div>
             <p>
              University President Lawrence S. Bacow declined to provide details on the circumstances that led to the departure of Cornel R. West 74, citing confidentiality policies, but defended Harvards existing tenure process in a Thursday interview.
             </p>

           <div class="subsection css-ws8bxy-Fi">
            <a href="/tag/scrutiny/" to="/tag/scrutiny/">
             Scrutiny

           </div>
           <h1 class="">
            <a href="/article/2021/3/18/louis-agassiz-scrut/" to="/article/2021/3/18/louis-agassiz-scrut/">
             Louis Agassiz, Under a Microscope
            </a>
           </h1>
           <div>
            <div class="contributor-container">
             <span class="byline">
              <a href="/writer/1215437/Saima_S._Iqbal/" to="/writer/1215437/Saima_S._Iqbal/">
               Saima S. Iqbal
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
            
           </div>
           <p>
            Though some historians argue it is difficult to reconcile these two visions of Louis Agassiz  one gentle and reverential, the other rigid and bigoted , they may simply be two sides of the same coin. Agassiz prided himself on his ability to distinguish and characterize species. With his theory of polygenism, he created taxonomies not only of turtles and jellyfish but also of human beings.
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="fm-article">
        <div class="css-7c03k-CleanParagraphs">

            </style>
            <div class="preview-image css-1j1ks1r">
            </div>
            <div class="preview-image css-uaxvn2-Object">
            </div>
           </a>
          </div>

           <div>
            <div class="contributor-container">
             <span class="byline">
              <a href="/writer/1216300/Gabrielle_J._Pesantez/" to="/writer/1216300/Gabrielle_J._Pesantez/">

              <a href="/writer/1216775/Rowena_N._Wilson-Olivo/" to="/writer/1216775/Rowena_N._Wilson-Olivo/">

              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
            
           </div>
           <p>
            Allanah R. J. Rolph 23-24, who grew up in rural South Dakota, is in the revision stages for a book focusing on the conflict between her progressive politics and the more conservative aspects of her upbringing.
           </p>

         <div class="preview-content">
          <h1 class="title-small">
           <a href="/article/2021/3/10/Victor-Crouin-Feature/" to="/article/2021/3/10/Victor-Crouin-Feature/">
            The Quarantine Crunch: Crouin Keeps His Eye on the Ball
           </a>
          </h1>
          <div>
           <div class="contributor-container">
            <span class="byline">
             <a href="/writer/1215343/Eliot__Min/" to="/writer/1215343/Eliot__Min/">
              Eliot Min
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
           
          </div>
          <p>
           Like many student-athletes at Harvard junior Victor Crouin had his world turned upside down when students were sent home in March due to the coronavirus pandemic. The star first seed on the Crimsons elite squash squad managed to return to his hometown of Marseille, France, just before the nation went into lockdown.
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="right-side" id="major-right-box">
       <div class="" id="topright-box">
        <div class="left-side">
         <div class="css-7c03k-CleanParagraphs">

             </div>
             <div class="preview-image css-uaxvn2-Object">
             </div>
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="preview-content">
            <h1 class="title-small">
             <a href="/article/2021/3/10/Noah-Kirkwood-In-Canada/" to="/article/2021/3/10/Noah-Kirkwood-In-Canada/">
              In Canada and Separated from Teammates, Noah Kirkwood Works to Stay Connected
             </a>
            </h1>
            <div>
             <div class="contributor-container">
              <span class="byline">
               <a href="/writer/1214555/Mahtab__Shihab/" to="/writer/1214555/Mahtab__Shihab/">
                Mahtab Shihab
               </a>
              </span>
             </div>
             
            </div>
            <p>
             He led the team in scoring 10 times and in assists 13 times during his sophomore campaign. Hoping to continue his impressive career, Kirkwood has been struggling to find adequate resources for training and playing basketball during the pandemic.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

            <h1 class="title-small">
             <a href="/article/2021/3/10/XC-in-AZ/" to="/article/2021/3/10/XC-in-AZ/">
              Uncharted Territory: Cross Country Runners Relocate to High Altitude for High-Volume Training
             </a>
            </h1>
            <div>
             <div class="contributor-container">
              <span class="byline">
               <a href="/writer/1214953/William__Connaughton/" to="/writer/1214953/William__Connaughton/">
                William Connaughton
               </a>
              </span>
             </div>
             
            </div>
            <p>
             The team hopped on a Zoom call over winter break and decided that they had to meet up somewhere. Training alone, scattered across different time zones, was too difficult for student-athletes to keep up their training volume and simply ruined team morale.
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="preview-content">

             Midfielder Lara Schenk Finds Ways to Train Among the Best Despite Pandemic
            </a>
           </h1>
           <div>
            <div class="contributor-container">
             <span class="byline">
              <a href="/writer/1215415/Zing__Gee/" to="/writer/1215415/Zing__Gee/">
               Zing Gee
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
            
           </div>
           <p>
            One year ago, as Harvard students were forced to vacate campus, junior midfielder Lara Schenk (#18) of the womens soccer team moved back home to Hannover, Germany. A Tuesday, March 10, 2020, email had announced that students would be required to vacate the campus by that Sunday, and the NCAA and all major sports would soon follow suit with shutdowns of their own.
           </p>
